  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着电子健康记录(EHRs)的普及，构建预测模型的关键挑战是确定最大化准确性的历史数据最优时间窗口，特别是针对髋膝关节置换术后30天再入院的预测。

Method: 研究分析了7,174名患者的超过400万次结构化就诊记录和8万条非结构化临床笔记，观察窗口从手术当天追溯至术前三年。采用词袋模型、TF-IDF、LDA等非神经编码器以及BERT、1D CNN、BiLSTM等神经编码器提取临床笔记特征，分别评估仅使用临床笔记、仅使用结构化数据以及融合两种模态的预测模型。

Result: 非结构化临床笔记的最优时间窗口显著短于结构化数据：仅术前3-6个月的笔记即可达到最大预测性能；而结构化数据的性能随时间窗口延长持续改善，但在12个月后严格趋于平稳。这种模态特异性时间模式在不同模型复杂度和编码器类型下保持一致。

Conclusion: 研究发现挑战了"更多历史数据必然产生更好预测"的普遍假设，为优化再入院预测模型建立了针对性的时间窗口指导原则，提示应根据数据类型选择合适的历史数据范围。

Abstract: With the proliferation of Electronic Health Records (EHRs), a critical challenge in building predictive models is determining the optimal historical data time window to maximize accuracy. This study investigates the impact of various observation windows ranging from the day of surgery to three years prior on predicting 30-day readmission following hip and knee arthroplasties. The dataset encompasses both structured encounter records (over 4 million) and unstructured clinical notes (80,000) from 7,174 patients. To extract meaning from the clinical notes, we employed a suite of non neural (BOW, count BOW, TF IDF, LDA) and neural encoders (BERT, 1D CNN, BiLSTM, Average). We subsequently evaluated models utilizing clinical notes alone, structured data alone, and a combination of both modalities. Our results demonstrate that the optimal time window for unstructured clinical notes is significantly shorter than for structured data, maximum predictive performance was achieved using notes from just three to six months prior to surgery. In contrast, performance using structured data improved as the time window lengthened, but strictly plateaued after twelve months. These modality-specific temporal patterns remained consistent regardless of model complexity or encoder type. Ultimately, these findings challenge the general assumption that more historical data inherently yields better machine learning predictions, establishing targeted time-window guidelines for optimizing readmission prediction models.

</details>


### [97] [SAVGO: Learning State-Action Value Geometry with Cosine Similarity for Continuous Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00787)
*Stavros Orfanoudakis,Pedro P. Vergara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出SAVGO算法，通过将基于价值的相似性融入动作空间的策略更新，统一了表示学习、价值估计和策略优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法虽利用表示学习提升强化学习样本效率，但很少直接用于动作空间的策略更新，存在研究空白。

Method: SAVGO学习联合状态-动作嵌入空间，使相似价值估计对具有高余弦相似度，生成动作相似性核，引导策略向更高价值区域改进。

Result: 在MuJoCo连续控制基准上，该方法在高维任务上超越强基线，消融研究验证了价值几何学习和相似性策略更新的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作通过几何一致性目标统一三个关键组件，在保持离策略演员-评论家训练可扩展性的同时实现性能提升。

Abstract: While representation and similarity learning have improved the sample efficiency of Reinforcement Learning (RL), they are rarely used to shape policy updates directly in the action space. To bridge this gap, a geometry-aware RL algorithm that explicitly incorporates value-based similarity into the policy update, State-Action Value Geometry Optimization (SAVGO), is proposed. In detail, SAVGO learns a joint state-action embedding space in which pairs with similar action-value estimates exhibit high cosine similarity, while dissimilar pairs are mapped to distinct directions. This learned geometry enables the generation of a similarity kernel over candidate actions sampled at each update, allowing policy improvement to be guided directly toward higher-value regions beyond local gradient-based updates. As a result, representation learning, value estimation, and policy optimization are unified within a single geometry-consistent objective, while preserving the scalability of off-policy actor-critic training. The proposed method is evaluated on standard MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks, demonstrating improvements over strong baselines on challenging high-dimensional tasks. Ablation studies are done to analyze the contributions of value-geometry learning and similarity-based policy updates.

</details>


### [98] [Generating Statistical Charts with Validation-Driven LLM Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00800)
*Pavlin G. Poličar,Andraž Pevcin,Blaž Zupan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个结构化LLM工作流，将图表生成分解为数据集筛选、绘图提案、代码合成、渲染、验证优化、描述生成和问答生成七个步骤，通过渲染输出验证解决可读性与语义不匹配问题。在UCI数据集上生成1500张图表和30003个问答对，评估16个多模态大模型，揭示图表语法问题已饱和，而数值提取、比较和推理仍具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从表格数据生成多样化可读图表对LLM仍是挑战，许多缺陷仅在渲染后显现且无法从数据或代码单独检测。现有数据集缺乏完全对齐的代码、上下文与问答对等工件，阻碍了图表生成过程的可检查性与多模态推理能力的系统性诊断研究。

Method: 设计七步结构化工作流：数据集筛选、绘图提案、代码合成、渲染、验证驱动的迭代优化、描述生成和问答生成。核心创新是引入渲染输出验证机制，针对性解决可视化特有的可读性与语义不匹配故障模式。将生成过程视为可检查流程而非一次性提示转代码，完整保留每张图表的代码、数据上下文、描述和问答对。

Result: 在UCI数据集上产出1500张图表（源自74个数据集，涵盖24种图表族），配套生成30003个问答对。对16个多模态大模型的评估表明，图表语法类问题性能接近饱和，而数值提取、比较和推理类任务仍存在显著挑战，验证了工作流在诊断模型能力方面的效用。

Conclusion: 该工作流不仅构建了高质量的图表-问答数据集，更提供了诊断图表 grounded 多模态推理的有效框架，清晰揭示了当前模型的强项与局限，为后续研究提供了可检查、可扩展的生成范式与基准测试平台。

Abstract: Generating diverse, readable statistical charts from tabular data remains challenging for LLMs, as many failures become apparent after rendering and are not detectable from data or code alone. Existing chart datasets also rarely provide fully aligned artifacts, such as executable code, dataset context, and question-answer pairs. We present a structured LLM-based workflow that decomposes chart generation into dataset screening, plot proposal, code synthesis, rendering, validation-driven refinement, description generation, and question-answer generation. By incorporating rendered-output validation, the workflow addresses visualization-specific failure modes such as readability and semantic mismatch. It treats chart generation as an inspectable process rather than a one-shot prompt-to-code task, retaining each chart with its code, dataset context, description, and question-answer pairs. Applied to UCI datasets, the workflow produces 1,500 charts from 74 datasets, spanning 24 chart families and paired with 30,003 question-answer pairs. We evaluate 16 multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) on these chart-question pairs. The results show that chart-syntax questions are nearly saturated, while value extraction, comparison, and reasoning remain more challenging, illustrating the workflow's utility for diagnostic studies of chart-grounded multimodal reasoning.

</details>

### [99] [AgentReputation: A Decentralized Agentic AI Reputation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00073)
*Mohd Sameen Chishti,Damilare Peter Oyinloye,Jingyue Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对去中心化AI智能体市场面临的声誉机制失效问题，提出AgentReputation框架。该框架通过三层分离架构（任务执行、声誉服务、防篡改持久化）、显式验证机制与声誉元数据关联、情境化声誉卡片防止跨域混淆，以及基于风险的自适应决策引擎，系统性地解决了智能体策略性操纵、能力不可迁移和验证标准不一等挑战，并规划了验证本体、隐私保护证据等未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化AI智能体市场为调试、补丁生成和安全审计等软件工程任务提供新范式，但现有声誉机制存在三重根本缺陷：智能体可策略性优化评估过程、已验证能力难以跨异构任务迁移、验证严谨性从轻量级自动化检查到昂贵专家审查差异巨大。现有联邦学习、区块链AI平台及LLM安全研究均无法同时应对这些挑战，亟需专门设计的去中心化声誉框架。

Method: 提出AgentReputation三层去中心化框架：1) 任务执行层负责实际任务处理；2) 声誉服务层提供显式验证机制（与声誉元数据绑定）和情境化声誉卡片（防止跨领域声誉混淆）；3) 防篡改持久层确保数据完整性。各层解耦以支持独立演进，并通过决策策略引擎实现基于风险与不确定性的资源分配、访问控制和自适应验证升级。

Result: 构建了完整的去中心化声誉基础设施，实现了：1) 三层分离的模块化架构；2) 可验证的声誉-验证关联机制；3) 任务情境感知的声誉表示方法；4) 动态风险评估驱动的决策引擎。该框架为去中心化AI市场提供了抗操纵、可迁移、可扩展的声誉管理解决方案。

Conclusion: AgentReputation通过创新的三层架构与情境化声誉机制，系统性地解决了去中心化AI智能体市场的声誉挑战。未来研究将聚焦于验证本体开发、验证强度量化、隐私保护证据机制、冷启动声誉引导及对抗性操纵防御等关键方向，以推动该框架在实践中的部署与应用。

Abstract: Decentralized, agentic AI marketplaces are rapidly emerging to support software engineering tasks such as debugging, patch generation, and security auditing, often operating without centralized oversight. However, existing reputation mechanisms fail in this setting for three fundamental reasons: agents can strategically optimize against evaluation procedures; demonstrated competence does not reliably transfer across heterogeneous task contexts; and verification rigor varies widely, from lightweight automated checks to costly expert review. Current approaches to reputation drawing on federated learning, blockchain-based AI platforms, and large language model safety research are unable to address these challenges in combination. We therefore propose \textbf{AgentReputation}, a decentralized, three-layer reputation framework for agentic AI systems. The framework separates task execution, reputation services, and tamper-proof persistence to both leverage their respective strengths and enable independent evolution. The framework introduces explicit verification regimes linked to agent reputation metadata, as well as context-conditioned reputation cards that prevent reputation conflation across domains and task types. In addition, AgentReputation provides a decision-facing policy engine that supports resource allocation, access control, and adaptive verification escalation based on risk and uncertainty. Building on this framework, we outline several future research directions, including the development of verification ontologies, methods for quantifying verification strength, privacy-preserving evidence mechanisms, cold-start reputation bootstrapping, and defenses against adversarial manipulation.

</details>


### [100] [Are Tools All We Need? Unveiling the Tool-Use Tax in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00136)
*Kaituo Zhang,Zhen Xiong,Mingyu Zhong,Zhimeng Jiang,Zhouyuan Yuan,Zhecheng Li,Ying Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文挑战工具增强推理始终优于原生思维链的共识，揭示在语义干扰环境下存在"工具使用税"现象，导致工具调用收益无法覆盖协议开销，并提出G-STEP门控机制以部分缓解性能退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管工具增强推理被广泛视为提升LLM智能体推理性能的有效途径，但其在不同噪声环境下的实际效果边界与代价尚未得到系统性分析，特别是在语义干扰条件下工具使用的性能变化规律仍不明确。

Method: 提出因子化干预框架，将工具使用总效应解耦为提示格式化成本、工具调用协议开销和实际执行增益三个独立因子，通过控制变量实验量化各组件贡献，并设计轻量级推理时门控机制G-STEP来抑制协议诱导的错误。

Result: 实验分析表明，在语义噪声环境下，工具执行带来的实际增益往往无法抵消"工具使用税"（即工具调用协议本身引入的性能退化）；G-STEP门控机制虽能部分恢复性能，但改善效果有限。

Conclusion: 工具增强推理并非总是有效，其性能表现受环境噪声影响显著；要实现根本性突破，需要从增强模型内在推理能力和工具交互能力入手，而非仅依赖协议优化。

Abstract: Tool-augmented reasoning has become a popular direction for LLM-based agents, and it is widely assumed to improve reasoning and reliability. However, we demonstrate that this consensus does not always hold: in the presence of semantic distractors, tool-augmented reasoning does not necessarily outperform native CoT. To explain this performance gap, we propose a Factorized Intervention Framework that isolates the cost of prompt formatting, the overhead of the tool-calling protocol, and the actual gain from executing tools. Our analysis reveals a critical tradeoff: under semantic noise, the gains from tools often fail to offset the "tool-use tax", which is the performance degradation introduced by the tool-calling protocol itself. To address this, we introduce G-STEP, a lightweight inference-time gate to mitigate protocol-induced errors. While this yields partial recovery, our findings suggest that more substantial improvements still require strengthening the model's intrinsic reasoning and tool-interaction capabilities.

</details>


### [101] [TUR-DPO: Topology- and Uncertainty-Aware Direct Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00224)
*Abdulhady Abas Abdullah,Fatemeh Daneshfar,Seyedali Mirjalili,Mourad Oussalah*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TUR-DPO是一种拓扑与不确定性感知的DPO变体，通过奖励答案推导过程而非仅结果，结合语义忠实度、效用和拓扑质量生成校准的不确定性信号，在不使用强化学习的情况下提升大语言模型的人类偏好对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLHF和DPO方法存在局限：DPO虽稳定且无需强化学习，但将偏好简化为扁平的胜负信号，对脆弱推理链产生的噪声或易碎偏好敏感，无法区分答案的推导过程质量。

Method: 提出TUR-DPO：1) 引出轻量级推理拓扑；2) 融合语义忠实度、效用性和拓扑质量构建校准的不确定性信号；3) 在这些信号上因子化可学习的小规模奖励；4) 将其融入不确定性加权的DPO目标函数，保持RL-free特性，仅依赖固定或移动参考策略。

Result: 在7-8B参数开源模型和数学推理、事实问答、摘要、有帮助/无害对话等基准测试上，TUR-DPO相比DPO显著提升评判胜率、忠实度和校准性，同时保持训练简洁性、避免在线采样。在推理密集型任务上匹敌或超越PPO，并在多模态和长上下文场景中保持一致性增益。

Conclusion: TUR-DPO通过拓扑与不确定性感知机制有效解决了DPO的扁平信号缺陷，在维持操作简洁性的同时实现更优的偏好对齐，特别在推理密集型任务中性能与PPO相当，为大语言模型对齐提供了更鲁棒且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences is commonly done via reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) or, more simply, via Direct Preference Optimization (DPO). While DPO is stable and RL-free, it treats preferences as flat winner vs. loser signals and is sensitive to noisy or brittle preferences arising from fragile chains of thought. We propose TUR-DPO, a topology- and uncertainty-aware variant of DPO that rewards how answers are derived, not only what they say, by eliciting lightweight reasoning topologies and combining semantic faithfulness, utility, and topology quality into a calibrated uncertainty signal. A small learnable reward is factorized over these signals and incorporated into an uncertainty-weighted DPO objective that remains RL-free and relies only on a fixed or moving reference policy. Empirically, across open 7-8B models and benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, factual question answering, summarization, and helpful/harmless dialogue, TUR-DPO improves judge win-rates, faithfulness, and calibration relative to DPO while preserving training simplicity and avoiding online rollouts. We further observe consistent gains in multimodal and long-context settings, and show that TUR-DPO matches or exceeds PPO on reasoning-centric tasks while maintaining operational simplicity.

</details>


### [102] [ARMOR 2025: A Military-Aligned Benchmark for Evaluating Large Language Model Safety Beyond Civilian Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00245)
*Sydney Johns,Heng Jin,Chaoyu Zhang,Y. Thomas Hou,Wenjing Lou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对军事决策支持对大型语言模型合规性评估的需求缺口，本研究提出ARMOR 2025基准。该基准基于战争法、交战规则与联合伦理条例三大军事 doctrine，利用OODA框架构建12类519个 doctrine-grounded prompts，对21个商业LLMs进行系统性测试，揭示了军事安全对齐的关键缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM安全基准聚焦通用社会风险，缺乏对军事法律伦理规则遵循能力的评估，无法满足军事行动 doctrine standards 的要求。随着LLMs在军事决策、协同与作战效能提升方面的应用潜力显现，亟需建立符合军事 doctrinal 要求的专用安全评估体系。

Method: 从战争法、交战规则、联合伦理条例三大军事法规源提取 doctrinal 文本，生成保持原义的多选题；采用OODA决策框架构建12类别 taxonomy；开发519个 doctrine-grounded prompts，对21个商业大模型进行系统性准确性与拒绝能力测试。

Result: 评估结果表明，21个被测商业LLMs在军事应用安全对齐方面存在关键缺陷，无法可靠遵循军事法律伦理规则，凸显了当前模型在军事场景下的安全脆弱性。

Conclusion: ARMOR 2025填补了军事领域LLM安全评估的空白，其 doctrine-grounded 与OODA结构化的方法论为军事AI应用提供了系统化的合规性测试工具，对确保军事决策支持系统的可靠性与合法性具有重要实践价值。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now being explored for defense applications that require reliable and legally compliant decision support. They also hold significant potential to enhance decision making, coordination, and operational efficiency in military contexts. These uses demand evaluation methods that reflect the doctrinal standards that guide real military operations. Existing safety benchmarks focus on general social risks and do not test whether models follow the legal and ethical rules that govern real military operations. To address this gap, we introduce ARMOR 2025, a military aligned safety benchmark grounded in three core military doctrines the Law of War, the Rules of Engagement, and the Joint Ethics Regulation. We extract doctrinal text from these sources and generate multiple choice questions that preserve the intended meaning of each rule. The benchmark is organized through a taxonomy informed by the Observe Orient Decide Act (OODA) decision making framework. This structure enables systematic testing of accuracy and refusal across military relevant decision types. This benchmark features a structured 12-category taxonomy, 519 doctrinally grounded prompts, and rigorous evaluation procedures applied to 21 commercial LLMs. Evaluation results reveal critical gaps in safety alignment for military applications.

</details>


### [103] [Causal Foundations of Collective Agency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00248)
*Frederik Hytting Jørgensen,Sebastian Weichwald,Lewis Hammond*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出基于因果博弈与因果抽象的集体智能体行为主义框架，用于形式化界定多智能体系统中集体智能体的形成条件，并应用于解决演员-评论家模型激励谜题及投票机制的集体智能体程度量化，为理解、预测和控制多智能体AI中的涌现集体智能体提供理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先进AI系统的安全性挑战在于多个简单智能体可能无意中形成能力与目标异于个体的集体智能体。更一般地，判断何时可将智能体群体视为统一集体智能体，是研究生物与人工系统中交互激励的基础性问题。

Method: 采用行为视角，将群体联合行动的理性目标导向预测模型能准确预测行为时，将其归为集体智能体。利用因果博弈（战略多智能体交互的因果模型）和因果抽象（高层模型对低层模型的忠实性形式化）进行形式化构建。

Result: 成功解决演员-评论家模型中的多智能体激励谜题，并对不同投票机制的集体智能体程度进行了定量评估。

Conclusion: 该框架旨在为理解、预测和控制多智能体AI系统中的涌现集体智能体奠定理论与实证基础。

Abstract: A key challenge for the safety of advanced AI systems is the possibility that multiple simpler agents might inadvertently form a collective agent with capabilities and goals distinct from those of any individual. More generally, determining when a group of agents can be viewed as a unified collective agent is a foundational question in the study of interactions and incentives in both biological and artificial systems. We adopt a behavioral perspective in answering this question, ascribing collective agency to a group when viewing the group's joint actions as rational and goal-directed successfully predicts its behavior. We formalize this perspective on collective agency using causal games -- which are causal models of strategic, multi-agent interactions -- and causal abstraction -- which formalizes when a simple, high-level model faithfully captures a more complex, low-level model. We use this framework to solve a puzzle regarding multi-agent incentives in actor-critic models and to make quantitative assessments of the degree of collective agency exhibited by different voting mechanisms. Our framework aims to provide a foundation for theoretical and empirical work to understand, predict, and control emergent collective agents in multi-agent AI systems.

</details>


### [104] [Token Arena: A Continuous Benchmark Unifying Energy and Cognition in AI Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00300)
*Yuxuan Gao,Megan Wang,Yi Ling Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出TokenArena——一个在端点粒度（而非模型/提供商级别）持续评估AI推理性能的基准测试框架。该框架从输出速度、首个令牌时间、工作负载混合价格、有效上下文和实时质量五个维度评估78个端点，并合成能耗、成本和保真度三项综合指标。研究发现同一模型在不同端点间性能差异巨大，且工作负载类型会彻底重塑性价比排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有公开推理基准仅在模型或提供商级别比较AI系统，但实际部署决策发生在端点级别——即包含提供商、模型、SKU以及具体量化、解码策略、区域和部署栈的元组。这种评估粒度与决策粒度的错配导致基准结果无法准确指导实际部署选择，亟需细粒度的端点级基准测试方法。

Method: 提出TokenArena框架，以端点为基本评估单位进行持续基准测试。具体测量五个核心轴：输出速度、首个令牌时间、工作负载混合价格、有效上下文长度和实时端点质量；并将这些指标与建模的能耗估算结合，合成三项综合指标：每正确回答的焦耳数、每正确回答的美元数和端点保真度（输出分布与第一方参考的相似度）。

Result: 在78个端点服务12个模型族的实证研究中，发现同一模型在不同端点间差异显著：数学和代码准确率最高相差12.5分，与第一方的指纹相似度差异达12分，尾部延迟相差一个数量级，每正确回答的建模能耗相差6.2倍。工作负载感知的混合定价彻底重排了排行榜：在聊天预设（3:1输入输出比）下前10的端点中，有7个在检索增强预设（20:1）下掉出前10；推理预设（1:5）则显著提升前沿闭源模型的排名，这些模型在聊天预设下因价格劣势被惩罚。

Conclusion: TokenArena是一个强调透明度和可复现性的方法论而非静态排名。研究发布了完整框架、schema、探测评估工具及v1.0排行榜快照，并公开了完整的数据来源和局限性，欢迎外部独立复现。该工作确立了端点级持续基准测试的必要性，为实际部署决策提供了更精准的评估工具。

Abstract: Public inference benchmarks compare AI systems at the model and provider level, but the unit at which deployment decisions are actually made is the endpoint: the (provider, model, stock-keeping-unit) tuple at which a specific quantization, decoding strategy, region, and serving stack is exposed. We introduce TokenArena, a continuous benchmark that measures inference at endpoint granularity along five core axes (output speed, time to first token, workload-blended price, effective context, and quality on the live endpoint) and synthesizes them, together with a modeled energy estimate, into three headline composites: joules per correct answer, dollars per correct answer, and endpoint fidelity (output-distribution similarity to a first-party reference). The framework's novelty is empirical and methodological. Across 78 endpoints serving 12 model families, the same model on different endpoints differs in mean accuracy by up to 12.5 points on math and code, in fingerprint similarity to first party by up to 12 points, in tail latency by an order of magnitude, and in modeled joules per correct answer by a factor of 6.2. We further show that workload-aware blended pricing reorders the leaderboard substantially: 7 of 10 top-ranked endpoints under the chat preset (3:1 input:output) fall out of the top 10 under the retrieval-augmented preset (20:1), and the reasoning preset (1:5) elevates frontier closed models that the chat preset penalizes on price. We release the framework, schema, probe and eval harness, and a v1.0 leaderboard snapshot under CC BY 4.0. TokenArena is a methodology, not a single ranking; we publish full provenance and limitations and welcome external replication.

</details>


### [105] [AgentFloor: How Far Up the tool use Ladder Can Small Open-Weight Models Go?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00334)
*Ranit Karmakar,Jayita Chatterjee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AgentFloor基准测试，通过30个确定性任务和16,542次实验评估16个开源模型与GPT-5，揭示中小型模型已能胜任大部分短周期结构化工具使用任务，而GPT-5仅在长期规划和约束追踪的复杂任务上略有优势，提出了"小模型处理常规动作，大模型专注深度规划"的智能体系统设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生产环境中智能体系统每个用户请求需多次调用模型，其中大部分为短周期、结构化的常规调用。现有评估无法回答关键问题：智能体工作流中哪些环节真正需要大型前沿模型，哪些可由较小模型高效处理。这一实践性路由问题促使作者探索模型能力边界，以优化系统效率与成本。

Method: 作者开发了AgentFloor基准测试，包含30个确定性任务，按六层能力阶梯组织，覆盖指令遵循、工具使用、多步协调及带持续约束的长期规划。在16个参数量0.27B至32B的开源模型以及GPT-5上进行评估，总计完成16,542次评分运行。

Result: 实验结果发现清晰的能力边界：1) 中小型开源模型已足够处理占实际智能体管线主导地位的短周期结构化工具使用任务；2) 最强开源模型整体表现与GPT-5相当，但运行成本显著更低、速度更快；3) 性能差距主要体现在需要持续协调和可靠约束追踪的长期规划任务，但双方可靠性均不理想；4) 该边界不能仅由模型规模解释，失败模式具有模型特异性而非普遍性。

Conclusion: 研究提出了智能体系统的实用设计原则：对常规操作广泛采用小型开源模型，仅对真正需要深度规划和控制的狭窄任务类别保留大型前沿模型。这一分层策略可显著提升成本效益，作者同时开源了基准测试工具、配置参数及完整运行数据集。

Abstract: Production agentic systems make many model calls per user request, and most of those calls are short, structured, and routine. This raises a practical routing question that existing evaluations do not directly answer: which parts of an agent workflow truly require large frontier intelligence, and which can be handled by smaller models? We introduce AgentFloor, a deterministic 30-task benchmark organized as a six-tier capability ladder, spanning instruction following, tool use, multi-step coordination, and long-horizon planning under persistent constraints. We evaluate 16 open-weight models, from 0.27B to 32B parameters, alongside GPT-5 across 16,542 scored runs. Our results reveal a clear boundary of model necessity. Small and mid-sized open-weight models are already sufficient for much of the short-horizon, structured tool use work that dominates real agent pipelines, and in aggregate, the strongest open-weight model matches GPT-5 on our benchmark while being substantially cheaper and faster to run. The gap appears most clearly on long-horizon planning tasks that require sustained coordination and reliable constraint tracking over many steps, where frontier models still hold an advantage, though neither side reaches strong reliability. We also find that this boundary is not explained by scale alone: some failures respond to targeted interventions, but the effects are model-specific rather than universal. These findings suggest a practical design principle for agentic systems: use smaller open-weight models for the broad base of routine actions, and reserve large frontier models for the narrower class of tasks that truly demand deeper planning and control. We release the benchmark, harness, sweep configurations, and full run corpus.

</details>


### [106] [Physically Native World Models: A Hamiltonian Perspective on Generative World Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00412)
*Sen Cui,Jingheng Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出哈密顿世界模型作为基于物理的建模范式，通过将观测编码为结构化潜相空间，利用哈密顿启发动力学进行演化，旨在解决现有世界模型在物理可靠性、动作可控性和长时稳定性方面的瓶颈，强调物理意义对决策预测的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前世界模型研究沿三条部分分离的路线发展（2D视频生成、3D场景重建、JEPA类潜模型），虽各有进展，但均难以实现物理可靠、动作可控且长时稳定的预测。核心瓶颈已从生成真实性转向物理意义与决策实用性。

Method: 提出哈密顿世界模型框架：将观测映射至结构化潜相空间，采用含控制、耗散和残差项的哈密顿启发动力学方程演化潜状态，解码生成未来观测序列，并用于规划决策。

Result: 理论分析表明哈密顿结构有望提升模型可解释性、数据效率及长时稳定性；但面临摩擦、接触、非保守力和可变形物体等实际机器人场景中的建模挑战，尚未提供实验验证。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于物理的世界建模提供了新范式，强调了物理基础对决策预测的关键作用，但实用化仍需解决复杂非理想物理效应的建模难题。

Abstract: World models have recently re-emerged as a central paradigm for embodied intelligence, robotics, autonomous driving, and model-based reinforcement learning. However, current world model research is often dominated by three partially separated routes: 2D video-generative models that emphasize visual future synthesis, 3D scene-centric models that emphasize spatial reconstruction, and JEPA-like latent models that emphasize abstract predictive representations. While each route has made important progress, they still struggle to provide physically reliable, action-controllable, and long-horizon stable predictions for embodied decision making. In this paper, we argue that the bottleneck of world models is no longer only whether they can generate realistic futures, but whether those futures are physically meaningful and useful for action. We propose \emph{Hamiltonian World Models} as a physically grounded perspective on world modeling. The key idea is to encode observations into a structured latent phase space, evolve the latent state through Hamiltonian-inspired dynamics with control, dissipation, and residual terms, decode the predicted trajectory into future observations, and use the resulting rollouts for planning. We discuss how Hamiltonian structure may improve interpretability, data efficiency, and long-horizon stability, while also noting practical challenges in real-world robotic scenes involving friction, contact, non-conservative forces, and deformable objects.

</details>


### [107] [Thinking in Text and Images: Interleaved Vision--Language Reasoning Traces for Long-Horizon Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00438)
*Jinkun Liu,Haohan Chi,Lingfeng Zhang,Yifan Xie,YuAn Wang,Long Chen,Hangjun Ye,Xiaoshuai Hao,Wenbo Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出IVLR框架，通过\trace{}这种交替包含文本子目标和视觉关键帧的显式中间表示，实现了长时序机器人操作的交错视觉-语言推理，在LIBERO基准上达到95.5%的平均成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言-动作策略存在模态割裂问题：纯文本思维链能编码因果逻辑但缺失空间约束，视觉预测提供几何线索但局限于局部且语义欠约束。长时序操作需要逻辑连贯且几何 grounded 的规划。

Method: 构建交错视觉-语言推理(IVLR)框架：1)设计\trace{}作为显式中间表示，在全任务时域内交替组织文本子目标与视觉关键帧；2)单模态多模态transformer从初始观测和指令自生成全局语义-几何轨迹；3)轨迹缓存并用于闭环动作解码；4)通过时序分割演示和VLM字幕生成伪监督信号，以弥补数据集缺乏此类轨迹的问题。

Result: 在LIBERO基准达95.5%平均成功率（长时序任务LIBERO-Long为92.4%），SimplerEnv-WidowX总体成功率59.4%。消融实验证实双模态必要性：无轨迹时LIBERO-Long降至37.7%，纯文本/纯视觉轨迹分别为62.0%/68.4%，完整交错轨迹达92.4%。压力测试显示可容忍局部损坏和执行漂移，但全局规划错误时性能受限。

Conclusion: IVLR通过显式交错语义-几何轨迹有效统一了文本的逻辑性与视觉的几何性，显著提升了长时序操作性能，展现了良好的局部鲁棒性，但整体性能仍依赖于轨迹的全局规划质量。

Abstract: Long-horizon robotic manipulation requires plans that are both logically coherent and geometrically grounded. Existing Vision-Language-Action policies usually hide planning in latent states or expose only one modality: text-only chain-of-thought encodes causal order but misses spatial constraints, while visual prediction provides geometric cues but often remains local and semantically underconstrained. We introduce Interleaved Vision--Language Reasoning (IVLR), a policy framework built around \trace{}, an explicit intermediate representation that alternates textual subgoals with visual keyframes over the full task horizon. At test time, a single native multimodal transformer self-generates this global semantic-geometric trace from the initial observation and instruction, caches it, and conditions a closed-loop action decoder on the trace, original instruction, and current observation. Because standard robot datasets lack such traces, we construct pseudo-supervision by temporally segmenting demonstrations and captioning each stage with a vision-language model. Across simulated benchmarks for long-horizon manipulation and visual distribution shift, \method{} reaches 95.5\% average success on LIBERO, including 92.4\% on LIBERO-Long, and 59.4\% overall success on SimplerEnv-WidowX. Ablations show that both modalities are necessary: without traces, LIBERO-Long success drops to 37.7\%; text-only and vision-only traces reach 62.0\% and 68.4\%, while the full interleaved trace reaches 92.4\%. Stress tests with execution perturbations and masked trace content show moderate degradation, suggesting that the trace can tolerate local corruption and moderate execution drift, but remains limited under stale or incorrect global plans.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合优化算法性能高度依赖参数设置，但单一全局配置难以适应不同实例的结构、需求模式和能源约束差异，在电动容量车辆路径问题中这种局限性尤为突出

Method: 采用离线调优获取实例特定参数标签，然后通过回归模型建立实例特征到参数的映射关系，实现对未知实例执行前的参数预测，研究对象为电动容量车辆路径问题的高级元启发式算法双级延迟接受爬山法

Abstract: Algorithm performance in combinatorial optimization is highly sensitive to parameter settings, while a single globally tuned configuration often fails to exploit the heterogeneity of instances. This limitation is particularly evident in the Electric Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem, where instances differ in structure, demand patterns, and energy constraints. This paper investigates instance-aware parameter configuration for Bilevel Late Acceptance Hill Climbing, a state-of-the-art metaheuristic for the Electric Capacitated Vehicle Routing Problem. An offline tuning procedure is used to obtain instance-specific parameter labels, which are then mapped from instance features via a regression model to enable parameter prediction for unseen instances prior to execution. Experimental results on the IEEE WCCI 2020 benchmark and its extensions show that the proposed approach achieves an average objective value reduction of $0.28\%$ across eight held-out test instances relative to a globally tuned configuration. This corresponds to a significant cost reduction in multimillion-dollar transportation operations.

### [109] [Learn where to Click from Yourself: On-Policy Self-Distillation for GUI Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00642)
*Yan Zhang,Daiqing Wu,Huawen Shen,Yu Zhou,Can Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了GUI-SD，首个专为GUI grounding设计的在策略自蒸馏框架。通过构建富含视觉信息的特权上下文和熵引导蒸馏机制，该方法在六个基准测试上均优于GRPO方法，同时提升了训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于GRPO的强化学习方法在GUI grounding任务上表现出色，但仍存在两大局限：依赖昂贵的多次轨迹采样，以及在困难样本上信号稀疏。OPSD虽能提供单轨迹的密集监督，但其在GUI grounding领域的应用尚未被探索。

Method: 提出GUI-SD框架，包含两个核心组件：1）使用目标边界框和高斯软掩码为教师模型构建视觉增强的特权上下文，提供丰富指导而不泄露精确坐标；2）采用熵引导蒸馏，根据数字重要性和教师置信度自适应加权token，聚焦于最具影响力和可靠性的位置进行优化。

Result: 在六个代表性GUI grounding基准测试上的广泛实验表明，GUI-SD在准确性和训练效率方面均持续优于基于GRPO的方法和朴素OPSD方法。

Conclusion: 该工作首次成功将OPSD应用于GUI grounding任务，通过创新的特权上下文构建和自适应蒸馏策略，有效解决了稀疏奖励和计算效率问题，为自主GUI智能体的发展提供了新思路。

Abstract: Graphical User Interface (GUI) grounding maps natural language instructions to the visual coordinates of target elements and serves as a core capability for autonomous GUI agents. Recent reinforcement learning methods (e.g., GRPO) have achieved strong performance, but they rely on expensive multiple rollouts and suffer from sparse signals on hard samples. These limitations make on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), which provides dense token-level supervision from a single rollout, a promising alternative. However, its applicability to GUI grounding remains unexplored. In this paper, we present GUI-SD, the first OPSD framework tailored for GUI grounding. First, it constructs a visually enriched privileged context for the teacher using a target bounding box and a Gaussian soft mask, providing informative guidance without leaking exact coordinates. Second, it employs entropy-guided distillation, which adaptively weights tokens based on digit significance and teacher confidence, concentrating optimization on the most impactful and reliable positions. Extensive experiments on six representative GUI grounding benchmarks show that GUI-SD consistently outperforms GRPO-based methods and naive OPSD in both accuracy and training efficiency. Code and training data are available at https://zhangyan-ucas.github.io/GUI-SD/.

</details>

### [110] [Intelligent Elastic Feature Fading: Enabling Model Retrain-Free Feature Efficiency Rollouts at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00324)
*Jieming Di,Xiaoyu Chen,Ying She,Siyu Wang,Lizzie Liu,Fenggang Wu,Jiaoying Mu,Tony Tsui,Amr Elroumy,Hsing Tang,Zewei Jiang,Qiao Yang,Lin Qi,Haibo Lin,Weifeng Cui,Daniel Li,Kapil Gupta,Shivendra Pratap Singh,Jie Zheng,Arnold Overwijk,Ling Leng,Sri Reddy,Robert Malkin,Rocky Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出智能弹性特征衰减(IEFF)系统，通过在生产环境服务时弹性控制特征覆盖率和分布，实现无需重训练的特征效率上线，将上线速度提升5倍，消除GPU开销，并减少50-55%的性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模排序系统依赖数千个用户行为特征，传统方法需要周期性的模型重训练，导致迭代周期长达3-6个月，消耗大量GPU资源，且上线吞吐量受限，阻碍了特征效率优化的敏捷性。

Method: IEFF是一种生产基础设施系统，通过在服务时弹性控制特征覆盖率和分布，支持增量式特征调整，利用持续训练使模型自适应，消除显式重训练依赖，同时内置严格安全护栏、可逆机制和全面监控。

Result: 在多个生产场景中，IEFF将效率相关上线加速5倍，消除重训练GPU开销，实现更快容量回收。离线和在线实验表明，渐进式特征衰减相比突然移除可防止50-55%的在线性能下降，同时保持模型行为稳定。

Conclusion: 弹性系统级特征衰减是管理现代工业排序系统特征效率的实用可扩展方案，实现了重训练-free的敏捷迭代，为工业界提供了稳定的特征生命周期管理基础设施。

Abstract: Large-scale ranking systems depend on thousands of features derived from user behavior across multiple time horizons. Typically requires model retraining -- resulting in long iteration cycles (3--6 months), substantial GPU resource consumption, and limited rollout throughput.
  We introduce Intelligent Elastic Feature Fading (IEFF), a production infrastructure system that enables retrain-free feature efficiency rollouts by elastically controlling feature coverage and distribution at serving time. IEFF supports incremental feature coverage adjustments while models adapt through recurring training, eliminating dependencies on explicit retraining cycles. The system incorporates strict safety guardrails, reversibility mechanisms, and comprehensive monitoring to ensure stability at scale.
  Across multiple production use cases, IEFF accelerates efficiency-related rollouts by 5$\times$, eliminates retraining-related GPU overhead, and enables faster capacity recycling. Extensive offline and online experiments demonstrate that gradual feature fading prevents 50--55\% of online performance degradation compared to abrupt feature removal, while maintaining stable model behavior. These results establish elastic, system-level feature fading as a practical and scalable approach for managing feature efficiency in modern industrial ranking systems.

</details>


### [111] [DynamicPO: Dynamic Preference Optimization for Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00327)
*Xingyu Hu,Kai Zhang,Jiancan Wu,Shuli Wang,Chi Wang,Wenshuai Chen,Yinhua Zhu,Haitao Wang,Xingxing Wang,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型推荐系统中多负样本偏好优化存在的偏好优化崩溃问题，本文提出DynamicPO框架，通过动态边界负样本选择和双边界动态beta调整机制，有效缓解梯度抑制现象，提升推荐精度且几乎无计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型推荐系统中，直接偏好优化(DPO)需借助多负样本目标函数来利用丰富的隐式反馈负样本并 sharpen 偏好边界。然而实证发现一个反直觉现象：增加负样本数量反而导致性能下降，尽管训练损失持续降低。理论分析表明这是由于易区分负样本压制了定义用户偏好边界的关键负样本的梯度，造成决策边界信号欠优化。

Method: 提出DynamicPO轻量级即插即用框架，包含两个自适应机制：(1) 动态边界负样本选择：识别并优先优化靠近模型决策边界的信息量大的负样本；(2) 双边界动态beta调整：根据边界模糊度逐样本校准优化强度，缓解梯度抑制问题。

Result: 在三个公开数据集上的广泛实验表明，DynamicPO能有效防止偏好优化崩溃，在多种多负样本偏好优化方法上显著提升推荐准确率，且计算开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: DynamicPO通过自适应聚焦边界关键负样本和动态调整优化强度，成功解决了多负样本场景下的偏好优化崩溃问题，为构建更鲁棒的LLM推荐系统提供了实用解决方案，代码已开源。

Abstract: In large language model (LLM)-based recommendation systems, direct preference optimization (DPO) effectively aligns recommendations with user preferences, requiring multi-negative objective functions to leverage abundant implicit-feedback negatives and sharpen preference boundaries. However, our empirical analyses reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon, preference optimization collapse, where increasing the number of negative samples can lead to performance degradation despite a continuously decreasing training loss. We further theoretically demonstrate that this collapse arises from gradient suppression, caused by the dominance of easily discriminable negatives over boundary-critical negatives that truly define user preference boundaries. As a result, boundary-relevant signals are under-optimized, weakening the model's decision boundary. Motivated by these observations, we propose DynamicPO (Dynamic Preference Optimization), a lightweight and plug-and-play framework comprising two adaptive mechanisms: Dynamic Boundary Negative Selection, which identifies and prioritizes informative negatives near the model's decision boundary, and Dual-Margin Dynamic beta Adjustment, which calibrates optimization strength per sample according to boundary ambiguity. Extensive experiments on three public datasets show that DynamicPO effectively prevents optimization collapse and improves recommendation accuracy on multi-negative preference optimization methods, with negligible computational overhead. Our code and datasets are available at https://github.com/xingyuHuxingyu/DynamicPO.

</details>


### [112] [Negative Data Mining for Contrastive Learning in Dense Retrieval at IKEA.com](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00353)

Method: 1) 结构化负采样策略：利用产品层级分类法和属性信息生成语义相近但相关性低的困难负样本；2) LLM评测方法：通过大语言模型为每个查询的所有候选产品分配相关性分数，替代传统人工标注；3) 基于宜家搜索引擎的延迟交互检索架构进行实现。

Conclusion: 困难负样本挖掘至关重要，但要弥合离线检索质量与在线用户参与度之间的鸿沟，必须将训练数据和离线评估基于真实用户搜索行为（包括查询意图分布和零点击模式）进行构建，而非仅依赖传统评测指标。

Abstract: Contrastive learning is a core component of modern retrieval systems, but its effectiveness heavily relies on the quality of negative examples used during training. In this work, we present a systematic approach to improving dense retrieval for IKEA product search through structured negative sampling strategies and scalable LLM-as-a-judge relevance evaluation.
  Building on IKEA Search Engine's late-interaction retrieval architectures, we introduce two key contributions: (1) structured negative sampling strategies that leverage product hierarchical taxonomy and product attributes to generate semantically challenging negatives, and (2) a comprehensive LLM-based evaluation methodology for generating training data. Rather than relying on sparse human annotations or random sampling, our LLM-based evaluation system allocates a score for all candidate products against each query.
  Our methodology achieves +2.6\% average category accuracy on offline real user query experiments on the Canada market. However, our A/B test on long-tail queries showed no statistically significant differences in user engagement metrics between the improved and baseline models ($p > 0.05$). We trace this gap to user search behavior: 67\% of popular searches exhibit zero-click rates above 50\%, indicating that a substantial proportion of search sessions result in no product engagement regardless of result ranking. These findings underscore the importance of hard negative mining but also the need for grounding training data and offline evals in real user search behavior -- including query intent distribution and zero-click patterns -- to bridge the gap between offline retrieval quality and online user engagement.

We therefore formalize Instruction-Following Table Retrieval (IFTR), a new task that requires models to jointly satisfy topical relevance and fine-grained instruction constraints. We identify two core challenges in IFTR: (i) sensitivity to content scope, such as inclusion and exclusion constraints, and (ii) awareness of schema-grounded requirements, including column semantics and representation granularity--capabilities largely absent in existing retrievers. We further propose a new metric, termed the Instruction Responsiveness Score, to evaluate whether retrieval rankings consistently adapt to user instructions relative to a topic-only baseline. Abstract: Next-basket recommendation (NBR) is a type of recommendation that aims to predict a set of items a user will purchase based on their historical transaction basket sequences. It is governed by a dynamic interplay between two distinct user intents: habitual repurchase, which involves repeating past behaviors, and exploratory interest, which involves discovering new items. However, existing NBR methods generally suffer from two limitations: (1) they often entangle these conflicting motives within a single representation, causing habits to overshadow discovery, and (2) they rely on discrete sequential modeling that ignores continuous-time intervals and item-specific periodicities. In this paper, we propose a novel solution named Time-Interval Disentangled Experts (TIDE) to address these challenges. TIDE incorporates a Hawkes-enhanced Fourier Time Encoding to capture item-specific temporal periodicities and dynamic decay. To decouple user intentions, TIDE utilizes a dual-expert architecture that integrates a Habit Expert for recurring needs and a Pattern-Guided Exploration Expert for discovery. Combined with an item-aware gating mechanism, TIDE adaptively balances repurchase and exploration. Extensive experiments on four diverse real-world datasets demonstrate that TIDE consistently outperforms representative state-of-the-art NBR methods.

Method: 本文通过提出一个四阶段IR挑战框架来概念化这一范式转变：从信息不可及（inaccessible）、不可发现（undiscoverable）、不匹配（misaligned）到不可验证（unverifiable）。同时，构建了一个按信息检索流程组织的信号噪声优化技术分类体系，涵盖索引、检索、上下文工程、验证和智能体工作流等环节。

Abstract: Modern information retrieval (IR) is no longer consumed primarily by humans but increasingly by large language models (LLMs) via retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and agentic search. Unlike human users, LLMs are constrained by limited attention budgets and are uniquely vulnerable to noise; misleading or irrelevant information is no longer just a nuisance, but a direct cause of hallucinations and reasoning failures. In this perspective paper, we argue that denoising-maximizing usable evidence density and verifiability within a context window-is becoming the primary bottleneck across the full information access pipeline. We conceptualize this paradigm shift through a four-stage framework of IR challenges: from inaccessible to undiscoverable, to misaligned, and finally to unverifiable. Furthermore, we provide a pipeline-organized taxonomy of signal-to-noise optimization techniques, spanning indexing, retrieval, context engineering, verification, and agentic workflow. ### [117] [A Replicability Study of XTR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00646)
*Rohan Jha,Reno Kriz,Benjamin Van Durme*

Main category: cs.IR

Method: 研究团队首先复现XTR检索算法及其修改的训练目标，然后将评估扩展到知识蒸馏训练框架和PLAID、WARP等高效检索引擎。通过控制变量对比实验，系统分析XTR在不同部署环境下的性能表现和机制原理。

Abstract: The XTR (conteXtual Token Retrieval) algorithm is a modification to ColBERT retrieval that avoids the costly step of fully gathering and reranking the candidates' embeddings by imputing their missing similarity scores from the initial token retrieval step. The original work proposes a modified training objective as necessary for effective XTR retrieval, arguing that standard ColBERT token scoring is unsuitable for imputation. In this paper, we replicate both the XTR retrieval algorithm and its modified training objective, and extend the evaluation to knowledge-distillation (KD) training and efficient retrieval engines (PLAID and WARP). We confirm the token-level matching characteristics claimed in the original work, but fail to replicate XTR's overall effectiveness advantage over ColBERT under a controlled comparison. We further show that XTR's training modification has a concrete mechanistic consequence for modern retrieval engines: by flattening ColBERT's characteristically peaked token score distribution, XTR training yields more discriminative centroid scores and thus more efficient IVF-based retrieval under PLAID and WARP. The utility of XTR training is therefore not limited to the low-$k'$ regime originally studied, but extends to any deployment setting where IVF-based engines are used. These findings offer practitioners concrete guidance on how and when to use XTR as their multi-vector retriever.

### [118] [Robust Multimodal Recommendation via Graph Retrieval-Enhanced Modality Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00670)
*Yuan Li,Jun Hu,Jiaxin Jiang,Bryan Hooi,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出GRE-MC框架，通过模态感知子图检索和图Transformer来解决多模态推荐中的模态缺失问题，在基准测试中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界中的多模态数据集常因传感器故障、标注稀缺或隐私限制而存在模态缺失问题，这严重降低了推荐系统的性能和可靠性。现有方法仅利用节点自身或邻居信息进行模态补全，忽略了图中丰富的语义上下文信息。

Method: 提出GRE-MC框架，包含三个核心组件：1) 模态感知子图检索机制，从全图中选择语义相关的子图；2) 图Transformer，通过全局注意力联合编码查询节点和检索到的子图；3) 可学习稀疏路由码本，将潜在嵌入规整为紧凑基以提高鲁棒性。

Result: 在多模态推荐基准数据集上的大量实验表明，GRE-MC持续优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: 子图检索和联合编码图Transformer的引入有效提升了模态补全的鲁棒性，验证了框架的有效性。

Abstract: Multimodal data plays a critical role in web-based recommendation systems, where information from diverse modalities such as vision and text enhances representation learning. However, real-world multimodal datasets often suffer from modality incompleteness due to sensor failures, annotation scarcity, or privacy constraints, which substantially degrade model performance and reliability. One effective solution to address this issue is modality completion, which reconstructs missing features to provide modality-complete graphs for downstream tasks. Given a query node with missing multimodal features, existing modality completion methods typically infer information from the node itself or its neighbors to reconstruct the missing modality. However, these methods may overlook semantically relevant context in the graph, which contains valuable cues that are non-trivial to capture through simple methods like neighborhood aggregation. In this work, we propose GRE-MC, a Graph Retrieval-Enhanced Modality Completion framework, to overcome these limitations. By introducing a modality-aware subgraph retrieval mechanism, GRE-MC selects semantically relevant subgraphs from the entire graph, providing richer contextual information for completing missing modalities. Subsequently, a graph transformer jointly encodes the query node and the retrieved subgraph via global attention to complete the missing features, while a learnable sparse-routing codebook regularizes latent embeddings into compact bases for improved robustness. Extensive experiments on multimodal recommendation benchmarks demonstrate that GRE-MC consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, validating the effectiveness of subgraph retrieval and joint-encoding graph transformer for robust modality completion.

### [119] [A Survey of Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Progress and Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00063)
*Yiyang Wei,Tingyu Song,Siyue Zhang,Yilun Zhao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文是关于推理密集型检索(RIR)的综述，针对相关性由潜在推理联系而非语义相似度决定的检索场景。文章为当前缺乏系统框架的碎片化领域提供了清晰的研究路线图，涵盖基准梳理、方法分类和未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型展现出涌现推理能力并已融入信息检索全流程，但RIR领域缺乏系统性框架来组织现有工作并明确未来方向，亟需整合当前零散研究进展。

Method: 本文采用三种系统化方法：1) 按知识领域和模态对现有RIR基准进行系统分类和详细分析；2) 基于推理在检索流程中的位置和方式建立结构化分类法，并分析其权衡与实践应用；3) 总结该领域的挑战与未来研究方向。

Result: 成果包括：当前RIR基准的系统化分析、推理集成方法的层次化分类框架、以及指导该领域未来发展的挑战与方向总结。

Conclusion: 该综述为这一快速增长但碎片化的RIR领域提供了清晰的研究路线图，通过系统梳理基准、方法和挑战，推动推理密集型检索技术的结构化发展。

Abstract: Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval (RIR) targets retrieval settings where relevance is mediated by latent inferential links between a query and supporting evidence, rather than semantic similarity. Motivated by the emergent reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), recent work integrates these capabilities into the IR field, spanning the entire pipeline from benchmarks to retrievers and rerankers. Despite this progress, the field lacks a systematic framework to organize current efforts and articulate a clear path forward. To provide a clear roadmap for this rapidly growing yet fragmented area, this survey (1) systematizes existing RIR benchmarks by knowledge domains and modalities, providing a detailed analysis of the current landscape; (2) introduces a structured taxonomy that categorizes methods based on where and how reasoning is integrated into the retrieval pipeline, alongside an analysis of their trade-offs and practical applications; and (3) summarizes challenges and future directions to guide research in this evolving field.

</details>
